hover:bg-neutrals-alpha-light-200 h-11 px-[22px] text-sm opsz-14 rounded-[6px]" href="/security-center">View Trust Center</a></div></div></div><div class="py-20 md:py-24 lg:py-[120px]"><div class="px-4 mx-auto max-w-[1536px]"><div class="rounded-2xl bg-neutrals-opaque-100"><div class="grid grid-cols-1 gap-y-6 gap-x-12 lg:grid-cols-2 lg:gap-x-16"><div class="flex flex-col p-4 lg:p-8 Paris</h4><blockquote class="mt-4 font-serif lg:mt-8 text-pullout-sm xl:text-pullout-md text-primary">&quot;<span>Our Glide app is by far the simplest and most powerful system we&#x27;ve used for vector-effect="none" stroke-linejoin="round"></path></svg></span></div><div class="sr-only"><div class=" lg:text-lg prose text-neutrals-opaque-700"><p class="mt-3">Glide is an intelligent no-code platform that lets you build custom, AI-powered business apps—without writing code. Operations teams use Glide to create logistics apps that track shipments, manage carriers, optimize routing, and replace manual spreadsheets. Apps are built using a simple visual interface and can connect to data sources like Google Sheets, Excel, and SQL databases.</p></div></div></button></div><div class="rounded-2xl mb-[6px] flex transition-colors duration-150 ease-[cubic-bezier(0.25, 0.1, 0.25, 1)] bg-neutrals-opaque-100 hover:bg-neutrals-opaque-200"><button class="text-left w-full px-6 pt-6 lg:pt-11 lg:px-11 pb-6 lg:pb-11"><div class="flex items-center justify-between"><p class="mb-1 font-sans text-left font-semibold text-md lg:text-lg text-black">How does logistics management software work?</p><span aria-label="Toggle FAQ" class="ml-2 text-neutrals-opaque-900"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="grow-0 transition rotate-180"><path d="M6 14L12 8L18 14" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" vector-effect="none" stroke-linejoin="round"></path></svg></span></div><div class="sr-only"><div class=" lg:text-lg prose text-neutrals-opaque-700"><p class="mt-3">Logistics management software helps you coordinate the movement of goods, monitor delivery timelines, and streamline transportation workflows. Instead of using disconnected spreadsheets or manual logs, modern tools like Glide let you centralize logistics data, automate processes, and gain real-time visibility across your supply chain. You can build custom apps that match your operations—from dispatch to delivery to carrier performance tracking.</p></div></div></button></div><div class="rounded-2xl mb-[6px] flex transition-colors duration-150 ease-[cubic-bezier(0.25, 0.1, 0.25, 1)] bg-neutrals-opaque-100 hover:bg-neutrals-opaque-200"><button class="text-left w-full px-6 pt-6 lg:pt-11 lg:px-11 pb-6 lg:pb-11"><div class="flex items-center justify-between"><p class="mb-1 font-sans text-left font-semibold text-md lg:text-lg text-black">Can I build a logistics app without coding experience?</p><span aria-label="Toggle FAQ" class="ml-2 text-neutrals-opaque-900"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="grow-0 transition rotate-180"><path d="M6 14L12 8L18 14" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" vector-effect="none" stroke-linejoin="round"></path></svg></span></div><div class="sr-only"><div class=" lg:text-lg prose text-neutrals-opaque-700"><p class="mt-3">Yes. With Glide, you don&#x27;t need to write a single line of code. Just connect your data and use pre-built components to create a custom logistics app. You can track shipments by status, location, or carrier, set up delivery notifications, and even capture proof of delivery—all without technical expertise.</p></div></div></button></div><div class="rounded-2xl mb-[6px] flex transition-colors duration-150 ease-[cubic-bezier(0.25, 0.1, 0.25, 1)] bg-neutrals-opaque-100 hover:bg-neutrals-opaque-200"><button class="text-left w-full px-6 pt-6 lg:pt-11 lg:px-11 pb-6 lg:pb-11"><div class="flex items-center justify-between"><p class="mb-1 font-sans text-left font-semibold text-md lg:text-lg text-black">How much does logistics management software cost?</p><span aria-label="Toggle FAQ" class="ml-2 text-neutrals-opaque-900"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="grow-0 transition rotate-180"><path d="M6 14L12 8L18 14" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" vector-effect="none" stroke-linejoin="round"></path></svg></span></div><div class="sr-only"><div class=" lg:text-lg prose text-neutrals-opaque-700"><p class="mt-3">Pricing varies based on features, scale, and users. With Glide, you can start for free and only pay as your needs grow. We offer a 14-day free trial of our <a class="underline" href="https://www.glideapps.com/pricing?version=businesses">Business plan</a>, which includes advanced functionality like Glide AI, Workflows, and additional data integrations.</p></div></div></button></div><div class="rounded-2xl mb-[6px] flex transition-colors duration-150 ease-[cubic-bezier(0.25, 0.1, 0.25, 1)] bg-neutrals-opaque-100 hover:bg-neutrals-opaque-200"><button class="text-left w-full px-6 pt-6 lg:pt-11 lg:px-11 pb-6 lg:pb-11"><div class="flex items-center justify-between"><p class="mb-1 font-sans text-left font-semibold text-md lg:text-lg text-black">What is the best software for logistics management?</p><span aria-label="Toggle FAQ" class="ml-2 text-neutrals-opaque-900"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="grow-0 transition rotate-180"><path d="M6 14L12 8L18 14" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" vector-effect="none" stroke-linejoin="round"></path></svg></span></div><div class="sr-only"><div class=" lg:text-lg prose text-neutrals-opaque-700"><p class="mt-3">The best logistics software depends on your operations and complexity. The key is choosing software that&#x27;s easy to use, flexible enough to match your process, and integrates with your existing systems.</p></div></div></button></div><div class="rounded-2xl mb-[6px] flex transition-colors duration-150 ease-[cubic-bezier(0.25, 0.1, 0.25, 1)] bg-neutrals-opaque-100 hover:bg-neutrals-opaque-200"><button class="text-left w-full px-6 pt-6 lg:pt-11 lg:px-11 pb-6 lg:pb-11"><div class="flex items-center justify-between"><p class="mb-1 font-sans text-left font-semibold text-md lg:text-lg text-black">What features should I look for in logistics software?</p><span aria-label="Toggle FAQ" class="ml-2 text-neutrals-opaque-900"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="grow-0 transition rotate-180"><path d="M6 14L12 8L18 14" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" vector-effect="none" stroke-linejoin="round"></path></svg></span></div><div class="sr-only"><div class=" lg:text-lg prose text-neutrals-opaque-700"><p class="mt-3">Important features to consider include:</p>
<ul>
<li>Real-time shipment tracking across carriers and lanes</li>
<li>Automated notifications for delays, exceptions, and deliveries</li>
<li>Route optimization and delivery scheduling</li>
<li>Proof of delivery capture and document uploads</li>
<li>Integration with spreadsheets, ERPs, and TMS platforms</li>
<li>Mobile access for drivers and field teams</li>
<li>Dashboards to monitor delivery performance, lead times, and more</li>
</ul>
<p class="mt-3">Look for software that adapts to your process—not the other way around.</p></div></div></button></div><div class="rounded-2xl mb-[6px] flex transition-colors duration-150 ease-[cubic-bezier(0.25, 0.1, 0.25, 1)] bg-neutrals-opaque-100 hover:bg-neutrals-opaque-200"><button class="text-left w-full px-6 pt-6 lg:pt-11 lg:px-11 pb-6 lg:pb-11"><div class="flex items-center justify-between"><p class="mb-1 font-sans text-left font-semibold text-md lg:text-lg text-black">Does Glide logistics software integrate with other tools?</p><span aria-label="Toggle FAQ" class="ml-2 text-neutrals-opaque-900"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="grow-0 transition rotate-180"><path d="M6 14L12 8L18 14" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" vector-effect="none" stroke-linejoin="round"></path></svg></span></div><div class="sr-only"><div class=" lg:text-lg prose text-neutrals-opaque-700"><p class="mt-3">Yes.
